 The first episode of Aamir Khan's television avatar Satyamev Jayate tried to awaken the society by raising a case of feticide
 to ham bhi aapako bataa den ki garbhadhaaran purv or prasav purv nidaan takanic adhinium kya kahata haih1
 Under the pre-conception and Pre-natal Diagnostic Techniques Act, 1994, it is a crime to perform pre-or post-conception gender selection and sex testing for female fetal murder before birth
 2
 Supporting and advertising for fetal testing is a legal offense
 iske tahat 3 se 5 saal tak kii jail va 10 hajaar se 1 lakh rupee tak kaa jurmaana ho saktaa he
 3
 garbhvatee stri kaa jabardasti garbhpaat karwaanaa aparaadh he
 Doing so can lead to life imprisonment
 4
 Under Section 313, a woman who undergoes an abortion without the consent of the pregnant woman can also be punished with life imprisonment or fine
 5
 Under section 314, if the woman dies due to the act done for the purpose of performing an abortion, then there can be ten years of imprisonment or fine or both
